       $j(document).ready(function(){

             interval: 250, // milliseconds delay before onMouseOver
             over: lv2_3_show, 
             timeout: 500, // milliseconds delay before onMouseOut
             out: lv2_3_hide
         });
 
     
         $j(".li_niveau2").hoverIntent({
             interval: 250, // milliseconds delay before onMouseOver
             over: lv3_show, 
             timeout: 500, // milliseconds delay before onMouseOut
             out: lv3_hide
         });

     function lv2_3_show(){ 
         $j(this).find('.conteneur_niveau2_3').slideToggle(0);
         $j(this).find('.lien_niveau1').addClass('hover_lien_niveau1')
     }
 
     function lv2_3_hide(){ 
         $j(this).find('.conteneur_niveau2_3').hide();
         $j(this).find('.lien_niveau1').removeClass('hover_lien_niveau1')
 
     }
